Select  I._RID_ INVRID, I.LOCATION_ID LOCID, 
              0 MQRID, 'N' MQSTATUS, (select count(*) from inventory where product_id='20815006' and location_ID=I.Location_ID )as Caseqty From
           INVENTORY I with(NOLOCK), LOCATIONS L with(NOLOCK),LOOKUP_VALUES LV with(NOLOCK) 
             Where I.LOCATION_ID  = L.LOCATION_ID              
             And L.VLEVEL = LV.VALUE      
				And LV.TABLE_NAME = 'COMMON' 
             And LV.FIELD_NAME='CASEPKLEVELSEQ'                         
            And PRODUCT_ID = '20815006'                           
             And L.TYPE != 'X'                                 
             And (RESERVATION_TYPE = '' OR RESERVATION_TYPE IS NULL) 
             And HOLD = 0 And RESERVED = 0                   
             And QUANTITY =24                       
            And Not Exists (Select 1 From Move_Queue M  Where 
            M.INV_RID = I._RID_ )

Select  I._RID_ INVRID, I.LOCATION_ID LOCID, 
              0 MQRID, 'N' MQSTATUS, (select count(*) from inventory where product_id='58515005' and location_ID=I.Location_ID )as Caseqty From
           INVENTORY I with(NOLOCK), LOCATIONS L with(NOLOCK),LOOKUP_VALUES LV with(NOLOCK) 
             Where I.LOCATION_ID  = L.LOCATION_ID              
             And L.VLEVEL = LV.VALUE      
				And LV.TABLE_NAME = 'COMMON' 
             And LV.FIELD_NAME='CASEPKLEVELSEQ'                         
            And PRODUCT_ID = '58515005'                           
             And L.TYPE != 'X'                                 
             And (RESERVATION_TYPE = '' OR RESERVATION_TYPE IS NULL) 
             And HOLD = 0 And RESERVED = 0                   
             And QUANTITY =24                       
            And Not Exists (Select 1 From Move_Queue M  Where 
            M.INV_RID = I._RID_ )

Select  I._RID_ INVRID, I.LOCATION_ID LOCID, 
              0 MQRID, 'N' MQSTATUS, (select count(*) from inventory where product_id='34615316' and location_ID=I.Location_ID )as Caseqty From
           INVENTORY I with(NOLOCK), LOCATIONS L with(NOLOCK),LOOKUP_VALUES LV with(NOLOCK) 
             Where I.LOCATION_ID  = L.LOCATION_ID              
             And L.VLEVEL = LV.VALUE      
				And LV.TABLE_NAME = 'COMMON' 
             And LV.FIELD_NAME='CASEPKLEVELSEQ'                         
            And PRODUCT_ID = '34615316'                           
             And L.TYPE != 'X'                                 
             And (RESERVATION_TYPE = '' OR RESERVATION_TYPE IS NULL) 
             And HOLD = 0 And RESERVED = 0                   
             And QUANTITY =24                       
            And Not Exists (Select 1 From Move_Queue M  Where 
            M.INV_RID = I._RID_ )
